     \xa{}{}{} {} {}{}\xb{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}     % {\meG}{\zeG}{\weG}{\rG}

     \xa{}{}{} {} {}{}\xb{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}{0}     % {\zeG}{\waG}{\riG}
